idle = {
	male = {
		default = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idle_entry" }

		AI_idle_infant = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idleInfant_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					# Warcraft
					scope:age <= age_5_value
				}
			}
		}

		AI_idle_child = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idleInfant_entry" }

				}
			}
		}

		AI_idle_basic = {

			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 99
					# Warcraft
					#scope:age >= age_10_value
					scope:current_weight <= 75
				}
			}
		}

		AI_idle_fat = {

		AI_honorable = {
			animation = { head = "AI_honorable_entry" torso = "AI_honorable_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0

					add = {
						value = 100
						add = scope:ai_honor
					}
					# Warcraft
					#scope:age >= age_10_value
					scope:ai_honor >= max_positive_honor
					scope:current_weight <= 50
					NOT = { is_dwarf_height = yes }

					portrait_mena_clothing_trigger = no

		AI_dishonorable = {
			animation = { head = "AI_dishonorable_entry" torso = "AI_dishonorable_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				# Score set to 100 + the inverse of the negative ai_value score (will range from 150 to 200)
				modifier = {
					add = {
						value = 100
						add = {
							value = ai_honor
							multiply = -1
						}
					}
					#scope:age >= age_10_value
					scope:ai_honor <= max_negative_honor
					scope:current_weight <= 20

				}
			}

				animations = AI_dishonorable_decal				# One or multiple portrait modifier overrides

# misc_pregnantSerious_entry (above) is for characeters with negative traits
#
# misc_pregnant_entry (below) is for characters with positive traits
#
# we had to put pregnant triggers all the way down here because we need to prioritize playing misc_pregnantSerious_entry. hence, you can find misc_pregnantSerious_entry above.
# 

		AI_pregnant_dwarf_or_armor = {
			animation = { head = "misc_pregnant_entry" torso = "misc_pregnantFat_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					OR = {
						is_dwarf_height = yes
						portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
					}
					portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant }
				}
			}
		}

		AI_pregnant = {
			animation = { head = "misc_pregnant_entry" torso = "misc_pregnant_entry" }

				base = 0

					add = 100
					portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant }
					NOT = { is_dwarf_height = yes }
				}
			}
		}
    }
	boy = male
	female = male
	girl = male

    male = { 
    		default = { head = "council_chancellor" torso = "council_chancellor" } 
		still = {

		}

			weight = {

admiration = {
	male = {
		default = { head = "emotion_admiration_entry" torso = "emotion_admiration_entry" }
		
		still = {
			animation = { head = "still" torso = "still" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 2000
					has_no_animations_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}

		portrait_modifier = {
			animations = emotion_admiration_decal
		}

		emotion_admiration = {
			animation = { head = "emotion_admiration_entry" torso = "emotion_admiration_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					AND = {
						scope:current_weight <= 50
						NOT = { is_dwarf_height = yes }
						NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		emotion_admiration_fat = {
			animation = { head = "emotion_admirationFat_entry" torso = "emotion_admirationFat_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					OR = {
						AND = { # Dwarf
							scope:current_weight <= 50
							is_dwarf_height = yes
							NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }                        
						}
						AND = { # Fat
							scope:current_weight >= 50
							NOT = { is_dwarf_height = yes }
							NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }
						}
					}					
				}
			}
		}

		emotion_admiration_fat_dwarf = {
			animation = { head = "emotion_admirationFatDwarf_entry" torso = "emotion_admirationFatDwarf_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					AND = {
						scope:current_weight >= 50
						is_dwarf_height = yes
						NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }                        
					}					
				}
			}
		}

		emotion_admiration_pregnant = {
			animation = { head = "misc_pregnant_entry" torso = "misc_pregnant_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					AND = {
						scope:current_weight < 45
						portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant }
						NOT = { is_dwarf_height = yes }
					}					
				}
			}
			portrait_modifier = {
				animations = emotion_happy_decal
			}
		}

		emotion_admiration_pregnant_dwarf = {
			animation = { head = "misc_pregnant_entry" torso = "misc_pregnantFat_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					AND = {
						scope:current_weight < 60
						portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant }
						is_dwarf_height = yes
					}					
				}
			}
			portrait_modifier = {
				animations = emotion_happy_decal
			}
		}

		emotion_admiration_pregnant_fat_dwarf = {
			animation = { head = "misc_pregnant_entry" torso = "misc_pregnantFatDwarf_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					AND = {
						scope:current_weight >= 60
						portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant }
						is_dwarf_height = yes
					}					
				}
			}
			portrait_modifier = {
				animations = emotion_happy_decal
			}
		}
	}
	boy = male
	female = male
	girl = male	
}

aggressive_spear = { # wields two handed spear
	male = {
		default = { head = "emotion_twoHandedAggressive1_entry" torso = "emotion_twoHandedAggressive1_entry" }
		
		still = {
			animation = { head = "still" torso = "still" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 2000
					has_no_animations_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
		emotion_two_handed_aggressive_spear_basic = {
			animation = { head = "emotion_twoHandedAggressive1_entry" torso = "emotion_twoHandedAggressive1_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					AND = {
						scope:current_weight <= 50
						NOT = { is_dwarf_height = yes }
						NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }
                        
					}
				}
			}
			portrait_modifier_pack = two_handed_spear
		}	

		emotion_two_handed_aggressive_spear_fat = {
			animation = { head = "emotion_twoHandedAggressive1_entry" torso = "emotion_twoHandedAggressiveFat1_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					OR = {
						AND = { # Dwarf
							scope:current_weight <= 50
							is_dwarf_height = yes
							NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }                        
						}
						AND = { # Fat
							scope:current_weight >= 50
							NOT = { is_dwarf_height = yes }
							NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }
						}
						AND = { # Muscular
							prowess >= 13
						}
						AND = { # Pregnant
							scope:current_weight < 45
							portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant }
							NOT = { is_dwarf_height = yes }
						}		
					}					
				}
			}
			portrait_modifier_pack = two_handed_spear
		}

		emotion_two_handed_aggressive_spear_fat_dwarf = {
			animation = { head = "emotion_twoHandedAggressive1_entry" torso = "emotion_twoHandedAggressiveFatDwarf1_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					OR = {
						AND = { # Fat Dwarf
							scope:current_weight >= 50
							is_dwarf_height = yes
							NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }                        
						}
						AND = { # Pregnant Dwarf
							scope:current_weight < 60
							portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant }
							is_dwarf_height = yes
						}	
						AND = { # Pregnant Fat Dwarf
							scope:current_weight >= 60
							portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant }
							is_dwarf_height = yes
						}		
					}
				}
			}
			portrait_modifier_pack = two_handed_spear
		}
	}
	boy = male
	female = male
	girl = male	
}

		default = { head = "emotion_schadenfreude" torso = "emotion_schadenfreude" }
		still = {
			animation = { head = "still" torso = "still" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 2000
					has_no_animations_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
		portrait_modifier = {
			animations = emotion_schadenfreude_decal
		}
	}
	female = male
	girl = male
	boy = male
}
